                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: সরল ছন্দিত স্পন্দনসম্পন্ন একটি কণার বিভিন্ন লেখচিত্র-<br>
(i) সরণ – সময় লেখচিত্র : সাইন সদৃশ<br>
(ii) বেগ – সময় লেখচিত্র : কোসাইন সদৃশ<br>
(iii) ত্বরণ – সময় লেখচিত্র : ঋণাত্মক সাইন সদৃশ<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৫৬৯]</p>
</span>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: সরল ছন্দিত স্পন্দনসম্পন্ন কণার সরণ ও ত্বরণের রাশিমালা&nbsp;<br>
যথাক্রমে,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-5-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>A</mi><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>s</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>i</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>n</mi><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi>&amp;#x03C9;</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>t</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-51" style="width: 5.371em;                                     <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: বল ধ্রুবকের মাত্রা <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-19-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>[</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>M</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>]</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-177" style="width: 3.158em; [ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৫৮১]</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: সরল দোলন গতিসম্পন্ন কোনো কণার সর্বোচ্চ গতিশক্তি, সর্বোচ্চ বিভবশক্তি এবং মোট শক্তি তিনটিই <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; position: relative; width: 2.215em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1001.19em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.613em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-405" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">9.81</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.24em, 1002.09em, 4.305em, -999.998em); top: -3.441em; left: 50%; margin-left: -1.064em;"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-406"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.092em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.363em, 1001.72em, 4.305em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-407"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-408" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-409" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">3.14</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-410" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.342em; left: 1.805em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-411" style="font-size: 50%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1002.22em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 2.215em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-412" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-413" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">0.993</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-414" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-415" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.215em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.948em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.353em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>π</mi><msqrt><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi></mfrac></msqrt><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi><msup><mi>π</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>9.81</mn><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>3.14</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>0.993</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-37">\rm \therefore T=2\pi\sqrt{\frac{L}{g}}\Rightarrow\ L=\frac{g}{\pi^2}=\frac{9.81}{\left(3.14\right)^2}=0.993\ m </script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৬০৩]</p>

=1.256\ s.</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৫৬৯]</p>

                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>সরল দোলন গতিসম্পন্ন কোনো কণার পর্যায়কাল বল ধ্রুবকের-</p>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>(i) <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-42-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>L</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-493" style="width: 2.953em; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.203em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mo>−</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-42">\rm L-T^2</script></span> লেখচিত্র: মূলবিন্দুগামী একটি সরলরেখার সমীকরণ।<br>
(ii) <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-43-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>g</mi><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-500" style="width: 2.871em; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.297em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.353em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi><mo>−</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-43">\rm g-T^2</script></span> লেখচিত্র: আয়তাকার অধিবৃত্ত।<br>
(iii) X-অক্ষের দিকে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-44-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>g</mi></mfrac></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-507" style="width: 0.781em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.617em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.986em, 1000.62em, 2.584em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-508"><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-509"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.494em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.33em, 4.305em, -999.998em); top: -3.686em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-511" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">g</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.647em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.752em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi></mfrac></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-44">\rm \frac{1}{g}</script></span> এবং Y-অক্ষের দিকে আনুষঙ্গিক <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-45-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-512" style="width: 1.15em;                                         <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p><span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-57-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi><mo>&amp;#x221D;</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msqrt><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>g</mi></msqrt></mfrac></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-707" style="width: 3.404em; top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-708"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-709" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">T</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-710" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">∝</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-711" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.068em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.95em, 4.387em, -999.998em); top: -3.686em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.449em;"><span class="msqrt" id="MathJax-Span-713"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.945em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.568em, 1000.33em, 4.305em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0.576em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-714"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-715" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">g</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.986em, 1000.37em, 1.232em, -999.998em); top: -1.555em; left: 0.576em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1001.07em, 1.191em, -999.998em); [ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৫৮৫]</p>

                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 31 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>একটি তরঙ্গের বেগ <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-58-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>3.1</mn><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>s</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-716" style="width: 4.547em; {\therefore L}_2-L_1=2.25 \ L_1-L_1=1.25 \ L_1</script></span><br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>পীড়ন ৩ প্রকার। যথা- দৈর্ঘ্য পীড়ন, আকার বা কৃন্তন বা মোচড় পীড়ন ও আয়তন পীড়ন।<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৪৯১]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

font-family: MathJax_Main; top: -4.014em; left: 0.207em;">−<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; padding-left: 0.166em;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1057" style="font-family: MathJax_AMS; padding-left: 0.289em;">∴</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1058" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">T</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1059" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">∝</span><span class="msqrt" id="MathJax-Span-1060" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.559em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.58em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0.822em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1061"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1062" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.609em, 1000.74em, 3.895em, -999.998em); top: -4.588em; left: 0.822em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.74em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; font-family: MathJax_Main; top: -4.014em; left: -0.08em;">−<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; font-family: MathJax_Main; top: -4.014em; left: 0.043em;">−<span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.076em, 1000.86em, 4.346em, -999.998em); top: -4.096em; left: 0em;"><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">√</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1063" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">.</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.215em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.897em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.302em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>π</mi><msqrt><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi></mfrac></msqrt><mo>;</mo><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mo>∴</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mo>∝</mo><msqrt><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></msqrt><mo>.</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-76">\rm T=2\pi\sqrt{\frac{L}{g}}; \ \therefore T\propto \sqrt L. </script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৬০৩]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>পয়সনের অনুপাত দুটি বিকৃতির অনুপাত, তাই এর কোনো মাত্রা ও একক নেই।<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা- ৫০৮]</p>
